<h2> <span class="mw-headline" id="General_Information">General Information</span></h2>
<div class="wi_body" style="width:100%">
<table border="0">

<tr>
<th class="wi_head">Work Title
</th>
<td class="wi_head" style="width:100%">Le nozze di Figaro
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th class="wi_head">Alt<span class="mh555">ernative</span><span class="ms555">.</span> Title
</th>
<td class="wi_head">The Marriage of Figaro
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th>Composer
</th>
<td><a href="/wiki/Category:Mozart,_Wolfgang_Amadeus" title="Category:Mozart, Wolfgang Amadeus">Mozart, Wolfgang Amadeus</a>
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th><span class="mh555">Opus/Catalogue Number</span><span class="ms555">Op./Cat. No.</span>
</th>
<td>K.492
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th><span class="mh555">I-Catalogue Number</span><span class="ms555">I-Cat. No.</span>
</th>
<td>IWM 348
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th><span class="mh555">Movements/Sections</span><span class="ms555">Mov'ts/Sec's</span>
</th>
<td>4 acts
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th><span class="mh555">Year/Date of Composition</span><span class="ms555">Y/D of Comp.</span>
</th>
<td>1786
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th>First Perf<span class="mh555">ormance</span><span class="ms555">.</span>
</th>
<td>1786-05-01 in Vienna: Burgtheater
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th>First Pub<span class="mh555">lication</span><span class="ms555">.</span>
</th>
<td>1796 - Bonn: Simrock, Plate 28 (vocal score)<br />1806-09 - Paris: Magasin du Musique, Plate 366* (full score)
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th>Librettist
</th>
<td><a href="/wiki/Category:Da_Ponte,_Lorenzo" title="Category:Da Ponte, Lorenzo">Lorenzo Da Ponte</a> (1749–1838)
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th>Language
</th>
<td>Italian
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th><span class="mh555">Composer Time Period</span><span class="ms555">Comp. Period</span>

<td><a href="/wiki/Category:Classical" title="Category:Classical">Classical</a>
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th>Piece Style
</th>
<td><a href="/wiki/Category:Classical_style" title="Category:Classical style">Classical</a>
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th>Instrumentation
</th>
<td>voices, mixed chorus, orchestra <div class="expandline" style="background-color:#E8E8E8;margin-left:0;margin-top:0;padding:0">
<dl><dd><i>Cast</i>
<dl><dd>Count Almaviva (baritone)<br />Countess Almaviva (soprano)<br />Susanna (soprano)<br />Figaro (bass)<br />Cherubino (soprano)<br />Marcellina (mezzo-soprano)<br />Barbarina (soprano)<br />Bartolo (bass)<br />Basilio (tenor)<br />Don Curzio (tenor)<br />Barbarina (soprano)<br />Antonio (bass)
</dd></dl>
</dd><dd><i>Mixed Chorus</i> (SATB)
<dl><dd>Peasants, Villagers, and Servants
</dd></dl>
</dd><dd><i>Orchestra</i>
<dl><dd>2 flutes, 2 oboes, 2 clarinets, 2 bassoons<br />2 horns, 2 trumpets, timpani, strings </div>
</dd></dl>
</dd></dl>
</td></tr>

<h2> <span class="mw-headline" id="Misc._Comments">Misc. Comments</span></h2>
<table class="collapsible" width="75%" align="center" style="font-size: 90%">

<tr>
<th colspan="2" align="center" style="background-color:rgb(250,190,135)"><b>Operas by <a href="/wiki/Category:Mozart,_Wolfgang_Amadeus" title="Category:Mozart, Wolfgang Amadeus">Wolfgang Amadeus Mozart</a></b>
</th></tr>
<tr>
<td valign="top" width="50%" style="background-color:rgb(250,220,180)">
